SPE'U BRTZIGS GRUB PA DANG, GOS SKU BKRAM PA'I G-YAS G-YON DU
RGYAL MTSAN DANG, MDUN DU MCHOD PA'I SPRIN RGYA CHEN PO SPOS, BLA
MA YAB SRAS DGE 'DUN TSOGS CHEN DANG BCAS PAS BCOM

LDAN 'DAS RDO RJE 'JIGS BYED KYI SGO NAS SBYIN SREG DANG RAB GNAS
RGYAS PAR MDZAD, DE'I TSE 'JA' 'OD SNA LNGAS NAM MKHA'I DBYINGS
GANG BA LAS ME TOG GI CHAR BAB PAS, DER 'KHOD PA'I SKYE BO MTHA'
DAG BLA MA YAB SRAS DANG GOS SKU LA SANGS RGYAS DNGOS KYI

'DU SHES DANG LDAN PAR GYUR TO, ,DE SKABS YAR KLUNGS SU SDE GZAR
LANGS PAR BRTEN, NANG SO 'PHYONG RGYAS BAS GDAN 'DREN SNGA PHYIR
BYUNG STE CHIBS KHA SKYUR, THOG MAR 'OL KHA BRGYUD, RONG CHAD
DKAR DU PHEBS GZHI LEN ZHABS TOG YANG DAG ZHUS,

RI SGOR MCHOD YON LHAN DU PHEBS, ZHAL NGO LA BKA' DBANG DANG
KHROM LA SPYI CHES SOGS GNANG, DE NAS RGYA RI RDZONG DU PHEBS TE,
MCHOG DMAN MTHA' DAG CHOS KYIS TSIM PAR MDZAD, CHAB TSAN GNANG
STE SLAR YANG CHOD DKAR DU PHEBS, ZHABS DRUNG RTZE NAS GDUNG

BRGYUD SKU GZHON PA'I DRUNG YANG MJAL BAL PHEBS, TSE DBANG; DPAL
MGON ZHAL GYI RJES GNANG STZAL, RIM PHYIS YAR KLUNGS TSA BA GRU
RU PHEBS, BKA' KHRAS BCAD 'PHYONG RGYAS ZHABS DRUNG DPON G-YOG CI
BDER THEGS CHOG PA SOGS DUS GZINGS RNAMS ZHI BAR
